### Fengtian Political Events ###
#################################

country_event = { #Rumors incite Regionalist Uproar
	id = fengtian.1
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event fengtian.1" }
	title = fengtian.1.t
	desc = fengtian.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CHI_official_announcement

	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = fengtian.1.a
		add_political_power = -20
		swap_ideas = {
			add_idea = FNG_Regionalist_Resentment
			remove_idea = FNG_Regionalist_Sentiment
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = fengtian.3
				days = 16
			}
			set_country_flag = regionalist_protest_1
		}
	}
}

####Suppress Regionalist Sentiment events###
country_event = { #Protests Continue REPEATING
	id = fengtian.3
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event fengtian.3" }
	title = fengtian.3.t
	desc = {
		text = fengtian.3.d1
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = regionalist_protest_1
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = fengtian.3.d2
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = regionalist_protest_2
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = fengtian.3.d3
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = regionalist_protest_3
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = fengtian.3.d4
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = regionalist_protest_4
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_CHI_protest

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_completed_focus = FNG_Silence_Targeted_Subversives
			has_completed_focus = FNG_Justify_Mass_Arrests
		}
	}

	option = { #Unfortunate but necessary
		name = fengtian.3.a
		add_political_power = -15
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = FNG_Regionalist_Resentment
				has_country_flag = regionalist_protest_3
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				add_idea = FNG_Regionalist_Outrage
				remove_idea = FNG_Regionalist_Resentment
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = regionalist_protest_1
				}
				clr_country_flag = regionalist_protest_1
				set_country_flag = regionalist_protest_2
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = regionalist_protest_2
				}
				clr_country_flag = regionalist_protest_2
				set_country_flag = regionalist_protest_3
				country_event = { # An Offer from the Kenpeitai
					id = fengtian.7
					days = 25
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = regionalist_protest_3
				}
				clr_country_flag = regionalist_protest_3
				set_country_flag = regionalist_protest_4
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = regionalist_protest_4
				}
				clr_country_flag = regionalist_protest_4
				set_country_flag = regionalist_protest_2
			}
			country_event = { # Repeating
				id = fengtian.3
				days = 20
				random = 600
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Agent Provocateurs in Action
	id = fengtian.4
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event fengtian.4" }
	title = fengtian.4.t
	desc = fengtian.4.d

	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Excellent
		name = fengtian.4.a
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = fengtian.5
				days = 7
			}
		}
		swap_ideas = {
			add_idea = FNG_Regionalist_Outrage
			remove_idea = FNG_Regionalist_Resentment
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #The Harbin Riots

	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event fengtian.5" }
	title = fengtian.5.t
	desc = fengtian.5.d

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Good... and bad.
		name = fengtian.5.a
		add_political_power = -30
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = fengtian.6
				days = 3
				random = 72
			}
		}
		885 = {
			damage_building = {
				type = infrastructure
				damage = 0.5
			}
		}
		886 = {
			damage_building = {
				type = infrastructure
				damage = 0.1
			}
		}
		714 = {
			damage_building = {
				type = infrastructure
				damage = 0.1
			}
		}
	}
}

		}

				limit = {

				}

					id = fengtian.8
					days = 18
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #An Offer from the Kempeitai
	id = fengtian.7
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event fengtian.7" }
	title = fengtian.7.t
	desc = fengtian.7.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_FNG_kempeitai

	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Take the deal
		name = fengtian.7.a
		complete_national_focus = FNG_Silence_Targeted_Subversives
		set_temp_variable = { CAPOP = 5 }
		FNG_CAPOP = yes
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 45
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = FNG_Regionalist_Resentment
					has_completed_focus = FNG_Justify_Mass_Arrests
				}
				country_event = {
					id = fengtian.8
					days = 18
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #No thank you
		name = fengtian.7.b
		add_political_power = 10
		set_temp_variable = { CAPOP = -1 }
		FNG_CAPOP = yes
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 55
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Regionalists suppressed
	id = fengtian.8
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event fengtian.8" }
	title = fengtian.8.t
	desc = fengtian.8.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_FNG_protest

	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		has_completed_focus = FNG_Justify_Mass_Arrests
		has_completed_focus = FNG_Silence_Targeted_Subversives
	}

	option = { #Progress
		name = fengtian.8.a
		add_political_power = 10
		set_country_flag = FNG_regionalists_suppressed
		remove_ideas = FNG_Regionalist_Resentment
	}
}

		}

			factor = 55

		add_war_support = -0.03

			factor = 45
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Railway Construction Jilin-Hailong

		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = fengtian.13.d_jap
		trigger = {
			FNG_JAP_hostile = no

				is_subject = no
			}
		}
	}

	picture = GFX_report_event_FNG_railway_map

	is_triggered_only = yes

		name = fengtian.13.a

		FNG_CAPOP = yes

			random_list = {
				20 = {

						id = fengtian.19
						days = 36
					}
				}

						id = fengtian.20
						days = 25
					}
				}

						days = 217
					}
				}
			}
		}

			factor = 55
		}
	}

				is_subject = no
			}

						days = 25
					}
				}

#Japanese Aid Cut#

country_event = { # Imperial Fury
	id = fengtian.22
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event fengtian.22" }
	title = fengtian.22.t
	desc = {
		text = fengtian.22.d
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				AND = {
					FNG_JAP_hostile = no
					JAP = {
						is_subject = no
					}
					market_liberal > 0
					market_liberal < 0.05
				}
				AND = {
					has_global_flag = fengtian_refuses_food
					has_global_flag = japan_punishes_fengtian
				}
				has_global_flag = fengtian_blames_japan
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = fengtian.22.d_influence_low
		trigger = {
			FNG_JAP_hostile = no
			JAP = {
				is_subject = no
			}
			market_liberal > 0
			market_liberal < 0.05
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = fengtian.22.d_fengtian_refuses_food
		trigger = {
			has_global_flag = fengtian_refuses_food
			has_global_flag = japan_punishes_fengtian
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = fengtian.22.d_fengtian_blames_japan
		trigger = {
			has_global_flag = fengtian_blames_japan
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_JAP_ultimatum

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 7
	}

	trigger = {
		tag = FNG
		FNG_JAP_hostile = no
		NOT = { has_global_flag = JAP_Fading_Sun }
		has_idea = FNG_The_Kwantung_Army
		NOT = {
			has_decision = FNG_Expel_Japanese_Officers
			has_idea = FNG_Japanese_Aid_Cut
			has_global_flag = FNG_projapan
		}
		OR = {
			AND = {
				market_liberal > 0.00
				market_liberal < 0.05
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #A hard lesson
		name = fengtian.22.a
		add_political_power = -50
		FNG_japan_cuts_aid = yes
		set_temp_variable = { CAPOP = 10 }
		FNG_CAPOP = yes
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 85
			modifier = {
				factor = 50
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = FNG_jap_path
					option = FNG_ASSERTIVENESS
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Expel their officers in retaliation!
		name = fengtian.22.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 15
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_war = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = JAP
					ratio < 1.0
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_country_flag = FNG_conference_begun
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = FNG_jap_path
						option = FNG_OBEDIENCE
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = FNG_jap_path
						option = FNG_YAMATO
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = FNG_jap_path
						option = FNG_MING
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = FNG_jap_path
						option = FNG_QING
					}
				}
			}
		}
		activate_decision = FNG_Expel_Japanese_Officers
		custom_effect_tooltip = FNG_expel_japanese_officers_tooltip
	}
}

country_event = { #Chosabu Intelligence 1
	id = fengtian.67
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event fengtian.67" }
	title = fengtian.67.t
	desc = fengtian.67.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_JAP_science

	trigger = {
		FNG_JAP_hostile = no
		NOT = { has_global_flag = JAP_Fading_Sun }
	}

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = fengtian.67.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { 
					has_dlc = "La Resistance"
				}
			}
			add_tech_bonus = {
				name = fengtian.67.t
				bonus = 0.66
				uses = 1
				category = decryption_tech
			}
		}
		else = {
			if = {
				limit = { 
					has_intelligence_agency = yes 
				}
				if = {
					limit = { 
						NOT = { 
							has_done_agency_upgrade = upgrade_commando_training 
						} 
					}
					upgrade_intelligence_agency = upgrade_commando_training
				}
				if = {
					limit = { 
						NOT = {
						has_done_agency_upgrade = upgrade_crypto_strength 
						}
					} 
					upgrade_intelligence_agency = upgrade_crypto_strength
				}
				if = {
					limit = { 
						NOT = { 
							has_done_agency_upgrade = upgrade_decryption_boost 
						} 
					}
					upgrade_intelligence_agency = upgrade_decryption_boost
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							has_done_agency_upgrade = upgrade_commando_training
							has_done_agency_upgrade = upgrade_crypto_strength
							has_done_agency_upgrade = upgrade_decryption_boost
						}
						NOT = { 
							has_done_agency_upgrade = upgrade_training_centers 
						}
					}
					upgrade_intelligence_agency = upgrade_training_centers
				}
			}
			else = {
				create_intelligence_agency = yes
				upgrade_intelligence_agency = upgrade_commando_training
				upgrade_intelligence_agency = upgrade_decryption_boost
			}
		}
	}
}

				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = FNG_jap_path
						option = FNG_OBEDIENCE
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = FNG_jap_path
						option = FNG_YAMATO
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = FNG_jap_path
						option = FNG_MING
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = FNG_jap_path
						option = FNG_QING
					}
				}
			}
		}
		add_political_power = 100
		set_global_flag = FNG_relations_JAP_broke
		set_potential_national_government = yes
		if = {
			limit = { is_in_faction_with = JAP }
			leave_faction = yes
		}
		diplomatic_relation = {
			country = JAP
			relation = non_aggression_pact
			active = no
		}
		diplomatic_relation = {
			country = JAP
			relation = military_access
			active = no
		}
		JAP = {
			diplomatic_relation = {
				country = FNG
				relation = guarantee
				active = no
			}
			diplomatic_relation = {
				country = FNG
				relation = military_access
				active = no
			}
		}
		declare_war_on = {
			target = JAP
			type = annex_everything
		}
		FNG_CA_remove = yes
		FNG_mantetsu_collapse = yes
	}
}

country_event = { #Escalate the Propaganda War
	id = fengtian.91
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event fengtian.91" }
	title = fengtian.91.t
	desc = {
		text = fengtian.91.d
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				FNG_mantetsu_level_high = yes
				FNG_mantetsu_level_very_high = yes
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = fengtian.91.d_mantetsu
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				FNG_mantetsu_level_high = yes
				FNG_mantetsu_level_very_high = yes
			}
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_CHI_ambassador_announcement

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = fengtian.91.a
		if = {
			limit = { FNG_mantetsu_level_very_high = yes }
			add_political_power = -50
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { FNG_mantetsu_level_high = yes }
			add_political_power = 10
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { FNG_mantetsu_level_medium = yes }
			add_political_power = 30
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { FNG_mantetsu_level_low = yes }
			add_political_power = 50
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { FNG_mantetsu_level_none = yes }
			add_political_power = 80
		}
	}
}

#Japan Weapons Import Events

country_event = { # Japan sends obsolete artillery
	id = fengtian.92
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event fengtian.92" }
	title = fengtian.92.t
	desc = fengtian.92.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_FNG_hiroshima_package

	trigger = {
		FNG_JAP_hostile = no
		NOT = { has_global_flag = JAP_Fading_Sun }
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = fengtian.92.a
		clr_country_flag = japan_equipment_request_active
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = { # ~1934
			type = artillery_equipment_1
			amount = 200
			producer = JAP
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Japan sends latest artillery
	id = fengtian.93
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event fengtian.93" }
	title = fengtian.93.t
	desc = fengtian.93.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_FNG_hiroshima_package

	trigger = {
		FNG_JAP_hostile = no
		NOT = { has_global_flag = JAP_Fading_Sun }
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = fengtian.93.a
		clr_country_flag = japan_equipment_request_active
		if = {
			limit = {
				JAP = {
					has_tech = artillery1
					NOT = {
						has_tech = artillery4
					}
				}
			}
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = { # ~1939
				type = artillery_equipment_2
				amount = 200
				producer = JAP
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				JAP = {
					has_tech = artillery4
				}
			}
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = { # 1942
				type = artillery_equipment_3
				amount = 200
				producer = JAP
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Japan artillery request
	id = fengtian.94
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event fengtian.94" }
	title = fengtian.94.t
	desc = {
		text = fengtian.94.d1
		trigger = {
			JAP = {
				OR = {
					has_equipment = {
						artillery_equipment_1 > 2000
					}
					has_equipment = {
						artillery_equipment_2 > 2000
					}
					has_equipment = {
						artillery_equipment_3 > 2000
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = fengtian.94.d2
		trigger = {
			JAP = {
				has_equipment = {
					artillery_equipment_1 < 2000
				}
				has_equipment = {
					artillery_equipment_2 < 2000
				}
				has_equipment = {
					artillery_equipment_3 < 2000
				}
			}
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_FNG_hiroshima_package

	trigger = {
		FNG_JAP_hostile = no
		NOT = { has_global_flag = JAP_Fading_Sun }
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # Send the latest equipment
		name = fengtian.94.a
		trigger = {
			JAP = {
				OR = {
					has_equipment = {
						artillery_equipment_1 > 2000
					}
					has_equipment = {
						artillery_equipment_2 > 2000
					}
					has_equipment = {
						artillery_equipment_3 > 2000
					}
				}
			}
		}
		FNG = {
			country_event = {
				id = fengtian.93
				days = 1
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				JAP = {
					has_tech = artillery1
					NOT = {
						has_tech = artillery4
					}
				}
			}
			JAP = {
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = { # ~1939
					type = artillery_equipment_2
					amount = -200
					producer = JAP
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				JAP = {
					has_tech = artillery4
				}
			}
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = { # ~1942
				type = artillery_equipment_3
				amount = -200
				producer = JAP
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
		}
	}

	option = { # Send Obsolete Equipment
		name = fengtian.94.b
		trigger = {
			JAP = {
				has_equipment = {
					artillery_equipment_1 > 499
				}
			}
		}
		FNG = {
			country_event = {
				id = fengtian.92
				days = 1
			}
		}
		JAP = {
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = { # ~1939
				type = artillery_equipment_1
				amount = -200
				producer = JAP
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
	}

	option = { # Refuse to send anything

					artillery_equipment_1 > 499
				}

					id = fengtian.107
					days = 14
				}
			}
			random_other_country = {

			}
		}
	}

country_event = { #Tang Yulin Tempts Fate
	id = fengtian.158
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event fengtian.158" }
	title = fengtian.158.t
	desc = fengtian.158.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CHI_warlord_battle

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		has_idea = FNG_Tang_Yulin_sec_pau
		controls_state = 610
		is_neighbor_of = MON
		MON = {
			controls_state = 612
		}
	}

	option = { #We must strike before they do!
		name = fengtian.158.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 20
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				country_exists = QIE #too risky
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					MON = { is_in_faction_with = RUS } #do not commit suicide
					MON = { is_guaranteed_by = RUS }
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					ROOT_is_threatened = yes
					MON = { default_attack_AI_trigger_FROM = yes }
					MON = { dont_start_major_faction_wars = yes }
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				MON = {
					is_ai = yes
				}
			}
			declare_war_on = {
				target = MON
				type = take_state
				generator = { 612 }
			}
			else = {
				MON = {
					country_event = fengtian.159
				}
			}
		}
		add_manpower = -1000
		set_temp_variable = { ZCPOP = 3 }
		FNG_ZCPOP = yes
	}

	option = { #Tang has done enough damage already!
		name = fengtian.158.b
		ai_chance = { base = 75 }
		MON = {
			country_event = fengtian.160
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = FNG_Tang_Yulin_sec_pau
			}
			remove_ideas = FNG_Tang_Yulin_sec_pau
		}
		add_political_power = -30
		add_manpower = -1000
		set_temp_variable = { ZCPOP = -3 }
		FNG_ZCPOP = yes
	}

	option = { #Maybe things will de-escalate
		name = fengtian.158.c
		ai_chance = { base = 5 }
		set_global_flag = MON_FNG_border_war
		MON = {
			country_event = {
				id = fengtian.161
				days = 2
			}
		}
		JAP = {
			country_event = {
				id = fengtian.162
				days = 2
			}
		}
		add_manpower = -5000
	}
}

country_event = { #Zongchang and Anqing prevent war hidden prep event, triggered by LEP-D anq.61
	id = fengtian.212
	hidden = yes

	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event fengtian.212"
		set_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc_started
		SQI = { #Zongchang controls at least one 5P state
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { state = 597 } #jinan west shandong
					NOT = { state = 1065 } #jiaodong north shandong
					NOT = { state = 1064 } #linyi south shandong
				}
				FNG = { add_to_array = { SQI_owned_league_states = PREV } }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { #checks if a proper state exists, if it does than indeed sqi owns 5P states
				any_of_scopes	= {
					array = SQI_owned_league_states
					is_owned_by = SQI
				}
			}


			for_each_scope_loop = {
				array = SQI_owned_league_states
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { state = 1047 }
						NOT = { state = 598 }
						NOT = { state = 1075 }
					}
					FNG = { add_to_array = { SQI_owned_crit_anq_states = PREV } }
				}
				else = {
					FNG = { add_to_array = { SQI_owned_jiangsu_states = PREV } }
				}
			}

			if = { #checks if a proper state exis, if yes than sqi owns 5P states crit by ANQ
				limit = {
					any_of_scopes = {
						array = SQI_owned_crit_anq_states
						is_owned_by = SQI
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc_sqi_controls_5p_crit_state
			}
			else = {
				set_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc_sqi_only_jiangsu
				SQI = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							OR = {
								controls_state = 1047
								controls_state = 598
								controls_state = 1075
							}
						}
						if = {
							limit = {
								NOT = { controls_state = 1047 }
							}
							FNG = {
								set_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc_sqi_notall_jiangsu
								add_to_array = { SQI_nonowned_jiangsu_states = 1047 } }
						}
						if = {
							limit = {
								NOT = { controls_state = 598 }
							}
							FNG = {
								set_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc_sqi_notall_jiangsu
								add_to_array = { SQI_nonowned_jiangsu_states = 598 } }
						}
						if = {
							limit = {
								NOT = { controls_state = 1075 }
							}
							FNG = {
								set_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc_sqi_notall_jiangsu
								add_to_array = { SQI_nonowned_jiangsu_states = 1075 } }
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			set_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc_sqi_only_shandong

		}

		country_event = {
			id = fengtian.213
			days = 1
		}
	}
}

						days = 1
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

country_event = { #
	id = fengtian.221
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event fengtian.221" }
	title = fengtian.221.t
	desc = fengtian.221.d

	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #
		name = fengtian.221.a
		set_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc_paccepted
		ANQ = {
			country_event = {
				id = anq.132
				days = 1
			}
		}
		SQI = {
			country_event = {
				id = shandong.36
				days = 1
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { ANQ = { has_country_flag = ANQ_lep_beat_chi } }
			country_event = {
				id = fengtian.225
				days = 14
			}
			ANQ = {
				country_event = {
					id = anq.136
					days = 11
				}
			}
			SQI = {
				country_event = {
					id = shandong.40
					days = 11
				}
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc_shd_inshandong
				NOT = { has_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc_sqi_only_shandong }
			}
			ANQ = {
				for_each_loop = {
					array = FNG.SQI_owned_league_states
					transfer_state = v
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc_shd_keepjiangsu
				NOT = { has_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc_sqi_only_jiangsu }
			}
			ANQ = {
				for_each_loop = {
					array = FNG.SQI_owned_crit_anq_states
					transfer_state = v
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc_shd_getjiangsu
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc_sqi_notall_jiangsu } }
				SQI = {
					transfer_state = 1047
					transfer_state = 598
					transfer_state = 1075
				}
			}
			else = {
				SQI = {
					for_each_loop = {
						array = FNG.SQI_nonowned_jiangsu_states
						transfer_state = v
					}
				}
				clr_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc_sqi_notall_jiangsu
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #
	id = fengtian.222
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event fengtian.222" }
	title = fengtian.222.t
	desc = fengtian.222.d

	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #
		name = fengtian.222.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc_shd_inshandong
				has_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc_anqgivejiangsu
				has_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc_sqi_only_shandong
			}
			#shandong only shandong, anq offers but fengtian doesnt
			set_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc_ideal_anqcedejiangsu
			SQI = {
				country_event = {
					id = shandong.37
					days = 1
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc_shd_inshandong
				NOT = { has_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc_anqall5p }
				NOT = { has_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc_sqi_only_shandong }
			}
			#all situations but shandong having only shandong			
			#if they have critical part, they keep all of jiangsu
			#if they have jiangsu parts, they keep those parts
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc_sqi_controls_5p_crit_state
				}
				set_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc_ideal_cedenonjiangsu
			}
			else = {
				set_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc_ideal_keepjiangsu
			}
			SQI = {
				country_event = {
					id = shandong.37
					days = 1
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc_shd_getjiangsu
				has_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc_sqi_notall_jiangsu
				NOT = { has_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc_sqiwantjiangsu }
			}
			#shandong part jiangsu, doesnt need rest jiangsu
			set_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc_ideal_keepjiangsu
			SQI = {
				country_event = {
					id = shandong.37
					days = 1
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc_shd_getjiangsu
				has_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc_sqi_only_shandong
			}
			#shandong only shandong, if anq is willing get all jiangsu, if not only xuhai potent
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc_anqgivejiangsu
				}
				set_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc_ideal_anqcedejiangsu
			}
			else = {
				set_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc_ideal_getxuhai
			}
			SQI = {
				country_event = {
					id = shandong.37
					days = 1
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc_shd_everything
				NOT = { has_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc_sqikeepall }
			}
			#shandong controls a crit state, but is actually willing to give up
			set_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc_ideal_keepjiangsu
			SQI = {
				country_event = {
					id = shandong.37
					days = 1
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			ANQ = {
				country_event = {
					id = anq.131
					days = 1
				}
			}
			SQI = {
				country_event = {
					id = shandong.35
					days = 1
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #
	id = fengtian.233
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event fengtian.233" }
	title = fengtian.233.t
	desc = fengtian.233.d

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #
		name = fengtian.233.a
		if = {
			limit = { tag = FNG }
			if = {
				limit = { 1047 = { is_controlled_by = SQI } }
				ANQ = { transfer_state = 1047 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { 598 = { is_controlled_by = SQI } }
				ANQ = { transfer_state = 598 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { 1075 = { is_controlled_by = SQI } }
				ANQ = { transfer_state = 1075 }
			}

			ANQ = {
				country_event = {
					id = fengtian.233
					days = 1
				}

					id = anq.64
					days = 4
				}
				set_country_flag = ANQ_sqi_is_ally

				give_resource_rights = { receiver = SQI state = 1047 }
				give_resource_rights = { receiver = SQI state = 598 }
				give_resource_rights = { receiver = SQI state = 1075 }
			}
			SQI = {
				country_event = {
					id = fengtian.233
					days = 1
				}

				set_variable = { SQI_jiangsu_exploitation_civ_factories = 1047.building_level@industrial_complex }
				add_to_variable = { SQI_jiangsu_exploitation_civ_factories = 598.building_level@industrial_complex }
				add_to_variable = { SQI_jiangsu_exploitation_civ_factories = 1075.building_level@industrial_complex }

				add_to_variable = { SQI_jiangsu_exploitation_mil_factories = 598.building_level@arms_factory }

					type = arms_factory
					level = SQI_jiangsu_exploitation_mil_factories
				}
			}

			1047 = {
				add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ANQ_jiangsu_shandong_deal_dynamic_modifier }
			}
			598 = {
				add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ANQ_jiangsu_shandong_deal_dynamic_modifier }
			}
			1075 = {
				add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ANQ_jiangsu_shandong_deal_dynamic_modifier }
			}
			597 = {
				add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = SQI_jiangsu_shandong_deal_dynamic_modifier }
			}

			set_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc2_success
			clr_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc_anqall5p
			clr_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc_anqgivejiangsu
			clr_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc_anqtheykeepjiangsu
			clr_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc_anqthreatzhang
			clr_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc_first_demands_heard
			clr_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc_ideal_anqcedejiangsu
			clr_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc_ideal_cedenonjiangsu
			clr_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc_ideal_getxuhai
			clr_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc_ideal_keepjiangsu
			clr_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc_p1_anqno

	title = fengtian.284.t

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = fengtian.284.a #yes
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				tag = SZC
				has_government = paternal_autocrat
			}
		}
		transfer_all_unit_leaders_to_FROM = yes
		for_each_scope_loop = {
			array = ROOT.subjects
			FROM = {
				set_autonomy = {
					target = PREV
					autonomy_state = kr_integrated_puppet
				}
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			annex_country = {
				target = ROOT
				transfer_troops = yes
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_ai = no
			}
			FROM = { change_tag_from = ROOT }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = fengtian.284.b #no
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 100
				tag = SZC
				has_government = paternal_autocrat
			}
		}
		leave_faction = yes
		FROM = {
			create_wargoal = {
				target = ROOT
				type = annex_everything
			}
		}
	}
}

	title = fengtian.2852.t
	desc = fengtian.2852.d

	picture = GFX_report_event_CHI_ambassador_announcement

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = fengtian.2852.a #Threaten them with war
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				add = -30
				has_elected_government = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -30
				OR = {
					any_enemy_country = {
						is_actual_major = yes
					}
					surrender_progress > 0.01
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -5
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = FROM
					ratio < 0.8
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -5
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = FROM
					ratio < 0.7
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -5
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = FROM
					ratio < 0.6
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -10
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = FROM
					ratio < 0.5
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				set_temp_variable = { FNG_japan_accept_chance = FROM.num_of_factories }
				subtract_from_temp_variable = { FNG_japan_accept_chance = ROOT.num_of_factories }
				divide_temp_variable = { FNG_japan_accept_chance = -3 }
				add = FNG_japan_accept_chance
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			set_country_flag = FNG_breakaway
			country_event = {
				id = fengtian.77
				days = 4
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = fengtian.2852.b #Accept
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 30
				has_elected_government = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 30
				OR = {
					any_enemy_country = {
						is_actual_major = yes
					}
					surrender_progress > 0.01
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 5
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = FROM
					ratio < 0.8
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 5
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = FROM
					ratio < 0.7
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 5
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = FROM
					ratio < 0.6
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 10
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = FROM
					ratio < 0.5
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				set_temp_variable = { FNG_japan_accept_chance = FROM.num_of_factories }
				subtract_from_temp_variable = { FNG_japan_accept_chance = ROOT.num_of_factories }
				divide_temp_variable = { FNG_japan_accept_chance = 3 }
				add = FNG_japan_accept_chance
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_china_claim_of_JAP = yes
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_variable = ambition_area_@ROOT }
					clear_variable = ambition_area_@ROOT
				}
				if = {
					limit = { is_claimed_by = ROOT }
					remove_claim_by = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
				OR = {
					is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT
					owner = {
						is_subject_of = ROOT
					}
				}
				OR = {
					is_core_of = FNG
					is_claimed_by = FNG
				}
				NOT = {
					state = 1075 #Nantong
					state = 996 #Weihaiwei
					state = 803 #Wenzhou
					state = 802 #Xiamen
					state = 801 #Shantou
					state = 747 #Fuzhou
					state = 746 #Ningbo
					state = 745 #Port Arthur
					state = 744 #Kiaochow
					state = 743 #Shanghai
					state = 729 #Macau
					state = 728 #Guangzhouwan
					state = 609 #Tianjin
					state = 592 #Guangzhou
					state = 326 #Hong Kong
				}
			}
			FNG = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}
		add_political_power = -100
		FROM = {
			country_event = {
				id = fengtian.2861
				days = 1
			}
		}
	}
}

			}

			hidden_effect = {
				set_political_party = {
					ideology = market_liberal
					popularity = 0.20
				}
				set_temp_variable = { CAPOP = 0 }
				FNG_CAPOP = yes
			}
		}
		else = {
			set_temp_variable = { CAPOP = -5 }
			FNG_CAPOP = yes
		}
		remove_ideas = FNG_The_Kwantung_Army
	}
}

country_event = { #Yuting Takes Over
	id = fengtian.299
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event fengtian.299" }
	title = fengtian.299.t
	desc = fengtian.299.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_JAP_conscription

	trigger = {
		FNG_JAP_hostile = no
		NOT = { has_global_flag = JAP_Fading_Sun }
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = fengtian.299.a
		#save popularities
		set_temp_variable = { FNG_totalist = FNG.party_popularity@totalist }
		set_temp_variable = { FNG_syndicalist = FNG.party_popularity@syndicalist }
		set_temp_variable = { FNG_radical_socialist = FNG.party_popularity@radical_socialist }
		set_temp_variable = { FNG_social_democrat = FNG.party_popularity@social_democrat }
		set_temp_variable = { FNG_social_liberal = FNG.party_popularity@social_liberal }
		set_temp_variable = { FNG_market_liberal = FNG.party_popularity@market_liberal }
		set_temp_variable = { FNG_social_conservative = FNG.party_popularity@social_conservative }
		set_temp_variable = { FNG_authoritarian_democrat = FNG.party_popularity@authoritarian_democrat }
		set_temp_variable = { FNG_paternal_autocrat = FNG.party_popularity@paternal_autocrat }
		set_temp_variable = { FNG_national_populist = FNG.party_popularity@national_populist }

		multiply_temp_variable = { FNG_totalist = 100 }
		multiply_temp_variable = { FNG_syndicalist = 100 }
		multiply_temp_variable = { FNG_radical_socialist = 100 }
		multiply_temp_variable = { FNG_social_democrat = 100 }
		multiply_temp_variable = { FNG_social_liberal = 100 }
		multiply_temp_variable = { FNG_market_liberal = 100 }
		multiply_temp_variable = { FNG_social_conservative = 100 }
		multiply_temp_variable = { FNG_authoritarian_democrat = 100 }
		multiply_temp_variable = { FNG_paternal_autocrat = 100 }
		multiply_temp_variable = { FNG_national_populist = 100 }

		#calculate marlib popularity
		set_temp_variable = { FNG_marlib_final_popularity = 100 }
		subtract_from_temp_variable = { FNG_marlib_final_popularity = FNG_totalist }
		subtract_from_temp_variable = { FNG_marlib_final_popularity = FNG_syndicalist }
		subtract_from_temp_variable = { FNG_marlib_final_popularity = FNG_radical_socialist }
		subtract_from_temp_variable = { FNG_marlib_final_popularity = FNG_social_democrat }
		subtract_from_temp_variable = { FNG_marlib_final_popularity = FNG_social_liberal }
		subtract_from_temp_variable = { FNG_marlib_final_popularity = FNG_social_conservative }
		subtract_from_temp_variable = { FNG_marlib_final_popularity = FNG_authoritarian_democrat }
		subtract_from_temp_variable = { FNG_marlib_final_popularity = FNG_national_populist }

		set_cosmetic_tag = FNG_JAP
		set_global_flag = FNG_projapan
		clr_country_flag = FNG_communications_clique_active
		clr_country_flag = FNG_recovery_league_active
		clr_country_flag = FNG_zhang_clique_active
		if = {
			limit = { has_war = yes }
			JAP = {
				country_event = {
					id = fengtian.301
					hours = 8
				}
				country_event = {
					id = fengtian.300
					days = 5
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			JAP = {
				country_event = {
					id = fengtian.300
					hours = 8
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_ideas = FNG_Assertive_Governance
			default_party_popularity_PP_gain = yes
			if = {
				limit = { has_unit_leader = 1101 }
				random_unit_leader = {
					limit = { has_id = 1101 }
					remove_unit_leader = yes
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_unit_leader = 11111 }
				random_unit_leader = {
					limit = { has_id = 11111 }
					remove_unit_leader = yes
				}
			}
			remove_all_ministers = yes
			add_ideas = {
				FNG_Yang_Yuting_hog_mli
				FNG_Yu_Zhishan_for_mli
				FNG_Ruan_Zhenduo_eco_mli
				FNG_Ding_Jianxiu_sec_mli
			}
			set_popularities = {
				totalist = FNG_totalist
				syndicalist = FNG_syndicalist
				radical_socialist = FNG_radical_socialist
				social_democrat = FNG_social_democrat
				social_liberal = FNG_social_liberal
				market_liberal = FNG_marlib_final_popularity
				social_conservative = FNG_social_conservative
				authoritarian_democrat = FNG_authoritarian_democrat
				paternal_autocrat = 0
				national_populist = FNG_national_populist
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = market_liberal
				elections_allowed = no
			}
			add_to_array = { global.asian_economic_sphere = FNG }
			add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = JAP_asian_economic_sphere_member }
			JAP_recalculate_economic_integration = yes
			FNG_recalculate_mantetsu_effects = yes
			unlock_national_focus = FNG_The_Question_of_the_Presidency
			country_event = { #Restoring Order to Manchuria
				id = fengtian.308
				days = 2
			}
			country_event = { #Monarchists in the concordia association
				id = fengtian.310
				days = 37
			}
			#country_event = {
			#	id = fngrebels.1
			#	days = 10
			#}
		}
		hidden_effect = { country_event = fngsystem.1000 }
	}
}

			factor = 50
		}
		if = {

			leave_faction = yes
		}
		add_political_power = 50
		add_stability = 0.05

		}

			factor = 50
		}
		if = {

			JAP = { add_to_faction = FNG }
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #DIRECT RULE FROM TOKYO(de jure)
	id = fngdynasty.3
	title = fngdynasty.3.t
	desc = fngdynasty.3.d

	picture = GFX_report_event_FNG_japanese_emperor

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = { #Those concordia guys aren't causing trouble
		name = fngdynasty.3.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		set_temp_variable = { CAPOP = 3 }
		FNG_CAPOP = yes
	}
	
	option = { #DIRECT RULE FROM TOKYO
		name = fngdynasty.3.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = FNG_direct_rule_tooltip
		set_country_flag = FNG_direct_rule
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = paternal_autocrat
			long_name = FNG_dynastic_japan_party_long
			name = FNG_dynastic_japan_party
		}
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = authoritarian_democrat
			long_name = FNG_dynastic_japan_party_long
			name = FNG_dynastic_japan_party
		}
		if = {
			limit = { JAP = { OR = { has_government = national_populist has_government = paternal_autocrat } } }
			set_politics = { ruling_party = paternal_autocrat }
		}
		else = {
			set_politics = { ruling_party = authoritarian_democrat }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = FNG_hirohito_emperor
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Hirohito"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/JAP/Portrait_JAP_Hirohito.png"
				expire = "1.1.1"
				ideology = authdem_pan_asianism_subtype
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Hirohito"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/JAP/Portrait_JAP_Hirohito.png"
				expire = "1.1.1"
				ideology = pataut_pan_asianism_subtype
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = FNG_chosen_kotohito_regent
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Kan'in Kotohito"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/FNG/Portrait_FNG_Kanin_Kotohito.png"
				expire = "1.1.1"
				ideology = authdem_pan_asianism_subtype
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Kan'in Kotohito"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/FNG/Portrait_FNG_Kanin_Kotohito.png"
				expire = "1.1.1"
				ideology = pataut_pan_asianism_subtype
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = FNG_chosen_yasuhito_regent
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Yasuhito"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/JAP/Portrait_JAP_Yasuhito.png"
				expire = "1.1.1"
				ideology = authdem_pan_asianism_subtype
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Yasuhito"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/JAP/Portrait_JAP_Yasuhito.png"
				expire = "1.1.1"
				ideology = pataut_pan_asianism_subtype
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_temp_variable = { CAPOP = party_popularity@market_liberal }
			set_temp_variable = { ZCPOP = party_popularity@paternal_autocrat }
			add_to_temp_variable = { ZCPOP = party_popularity@authoritarian_democrat }
			set_temp_variable = { RLPOP = party_popularity@national_populist }
			set_temp_variable = { temp = ZCPOP }
			add_popularity = { ideology = market_liberal popularity = -1 }
			add_popularity = { ideology = paternal_autocrat popularity = -1 }
			add_popularity = { ideology = authoritarian_democrat popularity = -1 }
			add_popularity = { ideology = national_populist popularity = -1 }
			
			multiply_temp_variable = { temp = 0.5 }
			add_to_temp_variable = { RLPOP = temp }
			
			set_temp_variable = { temp = ZCPOP }
			multiply_temp_variable = { temp = 0.8 }
			add_popularity = { ideology = radical_socialist popularity = temp }
			
			set_temp_variable = { temp = ZCPOP }
			multiply_temp_variable = { temp = 0.2 }
			add_popularity = { ideology = social_democrat popularity = temp }
			add_popularity = { ideology = social_liberal popularity = temp }
			
			add_popularity = { ideology = national_populist popularity = RLPOP }
			
			if = {
				limit = { JAP = { OR = { has_government = national_populist has_government = paternal_autocrat } } }
				add_popularity = { ideology = paternal_autocrat popularity = CAPOP }
			}
			else = {
				add_popularity = { ideology = authoritarian_democrat popularity = CAPOP }
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Unite the parties?
	id = fngnap.13
	title = fngnap.13.t
	desc = fngnap.13.d
	
	picture = GFX_report_event_FNG_big_party

	is_triggered_only = yes

	fire_only_once = yes
 
	option = { #ONE PARTY
		name = fngnap.13.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = authoritarian_democrat
			long_name = FNG_merged_zhang_party_long
			name = FNG_merged_zhang_party
		}
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = market_liberal
			long_name = FNG_merged_zhang_concordia_party_long
			name = FNG_merged_zhang_concordia_party
		}
		add_political_power = -150
		hidden_effect = {
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = social_democrat
				long_name = FNG_merged_zhang_party_long
				name = FNG_merged_zhang_party
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = social_liberal
				long_name = FNG_merged_zhang_party_long
				name = FNG_merged_zhang_party
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = social_conservative
				long_name = FNG_merged_zhang_party_long
				name = FNG_merged_zhang_party
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = FNG_concordia_association_active }
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = market_liberal
					long_name = FNG_merged_zhang_concordia_party_long
					name = FNG_merged_zhang_concordia_party
				}
			}
			else = {
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = market_liberal
					long_name = FNG_merged_zhang_party_long
					name = FNG_merged_zhang_party
				}
			}
			set_temp_variable = { CAPOP = party_popularity@market_liberal }
			add_popularity = { ideology = market_liberal popularity = -1 }
			add_popularity = { ideology = authoritarian_democrat popularity = 0.30 }
			add_popularity = { ideology = market_liberal popularity = CAPOP }
		}
	}
	
	option = { #Leave it be
		name = fngnap.13.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
		add_stability = 0.05
		country_event = {
			id = fngnap.14
			days = 13
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #fire new minister events
	id = fngsystem.0
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hidden = yes

	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_global_flag = FNG_projapan }
	}

	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event fngsystem.0"

		#Three month loop
		country_event = {
			id = fngsystem.0
			days = 60
			random = 150
		}
	}

	option = { #Recovery League
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = FNG_recovery_league_active
		}
		country_event = {
			id = fngsystem.1
			days = 5
			random = 120
		}
	}
	option = { #Communications Clique
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = FNG_communications_clique_active
		}
		country_event = {
			id = fngsystem.2
			days = 5
			random = 120
		}
	}
	option = { #Zhang Clique
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = FNG_zhang_clique_active
		}
		country_event = {
			id = fngsystem.3
			days = 5
			random = 120
		}
	}
	option = { #Concordia Association
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = FNG_concordia_association_active
		}
		country_event = {
			id = fngsystem.4
			days = 5
			random = 120
		}
	}
	#option = { #National Unity League
	#	trigger = {
	#		has_country_flag = FNG_national_unity_league_active
	#	}
	#	country_event = {

country_event = { #fire new minister events - RL
	id = fngsystem.1
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event fngsystem.1" }
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hidden = yes

	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_global_flag = FNG_projapan }
	}

	option = { #None
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
	}
	option = { #Foreign Minister
		trigger = {
			NOT = { ade_has_foreign_minister = yes }
		}
		country_event = fngpolitic.1
	}

	option = { #Economy Minister
		trigger = {
			authoritarian_democrat > 0.08
			ade_has_foreign_minister = yes
			NOT = { ade_has_economic_minister = yes }
		}
		country_event = fngpolitic.2
	}

	option = { #Interior Minister
		trigger = {
			authoritarian_democrat > 0.14
			ade_has_foreign_minister = yes
			ade_has_economic_minister = yes
			NOT = { ade_has_security_minister = yes }
		}
		country_event = fngpolitic.3
	}
}

	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event fngsystem.2" }

	}

			factor = 0
		}
	}

			NOT = { sco_has_economic_minister = yes }
		}
		country_event = fngpolitic.4
	}

	option = { #Foreign Minister
		trigger = {
			social_conservative > 0.08
			sco_has_economic_minister = yes
			NOT = { sco_has_foreign_minister = yes }
		}
		country_event = fngpolitic.5
	}

	option = { #Interior Minister
		trigger = {
			social_conservative > 0.14
			sco_has_economic_minister = yes
			NOT = { sco_has_security_minister = yes }
		}
		country_event = fngpolitic.6
	}
}

country_event = { #fire new minister events - ZC
	id = fngsystem.3
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event fngsystem.3" }
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hidden = yes

	trigger = {

	}

			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						AND = {
							has_country_flag = FNG_chosabu_radar_event_1
							has_country_flag = FNG_chosabu_radar_event_2
						}
						AND = {

							has_country_flag = FNG_chosabu_construction_event_2
						}

							has_country_flag = FNG_chosabu_efficiency_event_1
							has_country_flag = FNG_chosabu_efficiency_event_2
						}
						AND = {
							has_country_flag = FNG_chosabu_decryption_event_1
							has_country_flag = FNG_chosabu_decryption_event_2
						}
					}
				}
				clr_country_flag = FNG_chosabu_radar_event_1
				clr_country_flag = FNG_chosabu_radar_event_2
				clr_country_flag = FNG_chosabu_construction_event_1
				clr_country_flag = FNG_chosabu_construction_event_2
				clr_country_flag = FNG_chosabu_efficiency_event_1
				clr_country_flag = FNG_chosabu_efficiency_event_2
				clr_country_flag = FNG_chosabu_decryption_event_1
				clr_country_flag = FNG_chosabu_decryption_event_2
				#break = yes
			}
			country_event = {
				id = fngsystem.7
				days = 20
				random = 120
			}
		}
	}

	}
	option = { #Efficiency
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = chosabu_efficiency
		}
		country_event = fngsystem.10
	}
	option = { #Decryption
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = chosabu_decryption

	}

					}

						set_country_flag = Wang_Yitang_for_ade
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				random_list = {
					50 = {
						set_country_flag = Wu_Jinglian_for_ade
					}
					30 = {
						set_country_flag = Wang_Yitang_for_ade
					}
					20 = {
						set_country_flag = Huang_Fu_for_ade
					}

		}

						id = fengtian.24
						days = 36
					}
				}
				35 = {
					country_event = {
						id = fengtian.49
						days = 28
					}
				}
				30 = {}
			}
			random_list = {
				55 = {}
				45 = {
					country_event = { #Intelligence Leak
						id = fngpolitic.15
						days = 30
						random = 400
					}
				}
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { RLPOP = 2 }
		FNG_RLPOP = yes
	}

	option = { #Appoint Yitang
		name = fngpolitic.1.b
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = Wang_Yitang_for_ade
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 70
		}
		remove_ideas_with_trait = foreign_minister
		add_ideas = FNG_Wang_Yitang_for_ade

country_event = { #Encryption Codes Leaked!
	id = fngpolitic.15
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event fngpolitic.15" }
	title = fngpolitic.15.t
	desc = {
		text = fngpolitic.15.d_Wu
		trigger = {
			has_idea = FNG_Wu_Jinglian_for_ade
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = fngpolitic.15.d_Tang
		trigger = {
			has_idea = FNG_Tang_Yulin_sec_pau
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = fngpolitic.15.d_Ruan
		trigger = {
			has_idea = FNG_Ruan_Zhenduo_for_mli
		}
	}

	picture = GFX_report_event_FNG_harbin

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_idea = FNG_Wu_Jinglian_for_ade
			has_idea = FNG_Tang_Yulin_sec_pau
			has_idea = FNG_Ruan_Zhenduo_for_mli
		}
	}

	option = { #Damn!
		name = fngpolitic.15.a
		add_political_power = -20
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = FNG_Wu_Jinglian_for_ade
			}
			set_temp_variable = { RLPOP = -3 }
			FNG_RLPOP = yes
			set_temp_variable = { CAPOP = 1 }
			FNG_CAPOP = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = FNG_Tang_Yulin_sec_pau
			}
			set_temp_variable = { ZCPOP = -3 }
			FNG_ZCPOP = yes
			set_temp_variable = { CAPOP = 1 }
			FNG_CAPOP = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = FNG_Ruan_Zhenduo_for_mli
			}
			set_temp_variable = { CAPOP = 3 }
			FNG_CAPOP = yes
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					FNG = {
						any_enemy_country = { is_han_chinese_tag = yes }
					}
				}
				FNG = {
					random_enemy_country = {
						limit = { is_han_chinese_tag = yes }
						country_event = {
							id = fengtian.197
							days = 3
						}
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				random_other_country = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							is_neighbor_of = FNG
							tag = LEC
							AND = {
								tag = JAP
								is_subject = no
							}
						}
					}
					country_event = {
						id = fengtian.197
						days = 3
					}
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 60
		}
	}

	option = { #Remove him from office!
		name = fngpolitic.15.b
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = FNG_Wu_Jinglian_for_ade
			}
			remove_ideas = FNG_Wu_Jinglian_for_ade
			set_temp_variable = { RLPOP = -3 }
			FNG_RLPOP = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = FNG_Tang_Yulin_sec_pau
			}
			remove_ideas = FNG_Tang_Yulin_sec_pau
			set_temp_variable = { ZCPOP = -3 }
			FNG_ZCPOP = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = FNG_Ruan_Zhenduo_for_mli
			}
			remove_ideas = FNG_Ruan_Zhenduo_for_mli
			set_temp_variable = { CAPOP = -3 }
			FNG_CAPOP = yes
			set_temp_variable = { ZCPOP = 3 }
			FNG_ZCPOP = yes
			custom_effect_tooltip = FNG_japan_dislike
			set_country_flag = FNG_ruan_removed
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					FNG = {
						any_enemy_country = { is_han_chinese_tag = yes }
					}
				}
				FNG = {
					random_enemy_country = {
						limit = { is_han_chinese_tag = yes }
						country_event = {
							id = fengtian.197
							days = 3
						}
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				random_other_country = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							is_neighbor_of = FNG
							tag = LEC
							tag = JAP
						}
					}
					country_event = {
						id = fengtian.197
						days = 3
					}
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 40
		}
	}
}
